OpenSC O

mantishelp O

. O

Best O
( O
and O
therefore O
common O
) O
practice O
is O
to O
not O
display O
PHP O
error O
messages O
to O
the O
end O
user O
, O
severely O
limiting O
the O
applicability O
of O
this O
attack O
. O

Users O
running O
MantisBT O
on O
a O
vanilla O
nginx O
installation O
are O
unaffected O
because O
nginx O
will O
check O
to O
see O
whether O
the O
full O
URL O
path O
exists O
and O
is O
valid O
( O
with O
an O
XSS O
injection O
string O
, O
it O
won O
t O
be O
) O
. O

A O
suffix O
is O
appended O
, O
but O
can O
be O
stripped O
off O
using O
a O
null O
character O
( O
% O
00 O
) O
. O

Other O
web O
servers O
such O
as O
Apache O
won O
t O
perform O
these O
stringent O
checks O
and O
are O
therefore O
MantisBT O
is O
vulnerable O
to O
this O
attack O
when O
running O
on O
an O
Apache O
server O
. O

This O
attack O
does O
not O
require O
users O
to O
be O
authenticated O
or O
logged O
into O
a O
MantisBT O
installation O
to O
be O
impacted O
by O
this O
vulnerability O
. O
